                                   1567+*
                                   1568+* THIS ROUTINE IS USED TO FIND THE NEXT PARAMETER IN AN OPERAND FIELD.
                                   1569+* IF CALLER ENTERS AT GETOPRND, THIS ROUTINE SEARCHES FOR FIRST NON-
                                   1570+* BLANK.  IF CALLER ENTERS AT GETPARAM, SARG MUST POINT TO A NON-BLANK
                                   1571+*   THE CALLER MUST:  1. PASS RETURN ADDRESS IN REG 2
                                   1572+*                     2. PASS SARG ADDRESS IN REG 3
                                   1573+*                     3. PASS ADDRESS OF END OF FIELD + 1 IN REG 4
                                   1574+*
                                   1575+*   THIS ROUTINE WILL :  1. RETURN ALL REGS EXCEPT 3 & 5 UNCHANGED
                                   1576+*                        2. PLACE ACTUAL LENGTH OF PARAMETER IN REG 5
                                   1577+*                           IF SARG POINTS TO A COMMA, REG 5 IS ZERO
                                   1578+*                        3. REG 3 POINTS TO THE PARAMETER OR COMMA
                                   1579+*                        4. RETURN VIA REG 2 WHEN FIELD WAS EXHAUSTED
                                   1580+*                        5. RETURN VIA REG 2 + 4 WHEN SARG POINTS TO A
                                   1581+*                           COMMA
                                   1582+*                        6. RETURN VIA REG 2 + 8 WHEN SARG HAS FOUND
                                   1583+*                           THE PARAMETER
